   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

     1    /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001
     2    /*********************************************************************/00000002
     3    /*                                                                   */00000003
     4    /* NAME: MAP3270 - SCREEN COMPILER                                   */00000004
     5    /*                                                                   */00000005
     6    /*********************************************************************/00000006
     7    /*                                                                   */00000007
     8    /*  (C) COPYRIGHT 2009  CEDAR LAKE EMPORIUM LLC   ALL RIGHTS RESERVED*/00000008
     9    /*  (C) COPYRIGHT 2010  CEDAR LAKE EMPORIUM LLC   ALL RIGHTS RESERVED*/00000009
    10    /*                                                                   */00000010
    11    /*  THIS SOURCE CODE AS WELL AS ANY OBJECT CODE RESULTING FROM THIS  */00000011
    12    /*  SOURCE CODE MAY BE DISTRIBUTED FREELY PROVIDED NO FEE IS CHARGED */00000012
    13    /*  AND FOR NON-COMERCIAL PURPOSES.                                  */00000013
    14    /*                                                                   */00000014
    15    /*  FOR COMMERCIAL DISTRIBUTION RIGHTS, CONTACT THE COPYRIGHT OWNER. */00000015
    16    /*                                                                   */00000016
    17    /*********************************************************************/00000017
    18    /*                                                                   */00000018
    19    /* THIS IS A PROGRAM TO PROCESS A SCREEN DEFINITION FILE AND CREATES */00000019
    20    /* A PANEL FOR THE MAP3270 SYSTEM.                                   */00000020
    21    /*                                                                   */00000021
    22    /* A PANEL FOR THE MAP3270 SYSTEM CONSISTS OF 2 COMPONENTS - A       */00000022
    23    /* PHYSICAL MAP AND A USER MAP.  CONCEPTUALLY THESE ARE LIKE CICS    */00000023
    24    /* PHYSICAL AND SYMBOLIC MAPS.  HOWEVER, THERE IS NO COMPATABILITY.  */00000024
    25    /*                                                                   */00000025
    26    /* THE PHYSICAL MAP IS CONSISTS OF AN INDEX, THE ACTUAL 3270 MAP     */00000026
    27    /* AND THE CROSS REFERENCE FROM THE PHYSICAL MAP TO A USER MAP.      */00000027
    28    /* THE USER MAP IS THE AREA THAT USER'S APPLICATION SENDS AND        */00000028
    29    /* RECEIVES DATA FROM MAP3270 RUNTIME MODULES.                       */00000029
    30    /*                                                                   */00000030
    31    /* USER MAPS ARE GENERATED FOR ASSEMBLER, COBOL, AND PL/I (F).       */00000031
    32    /* THE PHYSICAL MAP IS GENERATED AND MUST BE ASSEMLED AND LINKED.    */00000032
    33    /*                                                                   */00000033
    34    /* REVISION HISTORY                                                  */00000034
    35    /* ------  --------------------------------------------------------  */00000035
    36    /* V2.0.0  "DOWNGRADED" FROM PL/1 OPTIMIZING COMPILER TO PL/1 (F)    */00000036
    37    /*         SEPT 2008                                                 */00000037
    38    /* V2.1.0  ADDED SUPPORT FOR THE EXTENTED ATTRIBUTES HIGHLITE AND    */00000038
    39    /*         COLOR.                                                    */00000039
    40    /*         REWORKED CODE TO USE THE SELECT...WHEN  MACRO, WHICH      */00000040
    41    /*         SIMULATES THE SELECT STATEMENT.                           */00000041
    42    /*         AUGUST 2010                                               */00000042
    43    /*                                                                   */00000043
    44    /*********************************************************************/00000044

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE      3

    46    MAPGEN:PROC OPTIONS(MAIN);                                             00000046
    47       DECLARE (PANEL,ASM,COB,PL1)                                         00000047
    48                STREAM OUTPUT FILE;                                        00000048
    49       DECLARE  PANEL_SEQ              FIXED DEC(9,2) INIT(1);             00000049
    50       DECLARE  NOT_E_O_F              BIT(1) ALIGNED;                     00000050
    51       DECLARE  NO_ATTRIB              BIT(1) ALIGNED;                     00000051
    52       DECLARE  PANEL_NAME             CHAR(7) VARYING INIT('PANELNM');    00000052
    53       DECLARE  MY_REC                 CHAR(80);                           00000053
    54       DECLARE  PROCESS_STATUS         CHAR(7);                            00000054
    55       DECLARE  SCR_IMG(26)            CHAR(82);                           00000055
    56       DECLARE  ERROR_FOUND            BIT(1) ALIGNED INIT('0'B),          00000056
    57                IHESARC                ENTRY(FIXED BIN(31,0)),             00000057
    58                RETURN_CODE            FIXED BIN(31,0) ALIGNED INIT(0);    00000058


    59    /*********************************************************************/00000059

    70                  2 TITLE              BIT(1) ALIGNED,                     00000070
    71                  2 STOP_BIT           BIT(1) ALIGNED,                     00000071
    72                  2 CUR                BIT(1) ALIGNED,                     00000072

    74                  2 COLOR              CHAR(3);                            00000074

    86                  2 FLD_ATTR           FIXED BINARY(15),                   00000086

   106               PGM_VER                 CHAR(8) STATIC INIT('V2.1.0  ');    00000106

   118       DECLARE VAR_CTR                 FIXED BINARY(15);                   00000118

   120               PAGE_NO                 FIXED DEC(3,0) INIT(0),             00000120

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE      8



   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   123    /*********************************************************************/00000123
   124    /*                                                                   */00000124
   125    /* READ AND LIST THE INPUT STATEMENTS.  SET UP THE PAGE HEADING      */00000125
   126    /*    SET UP THE PAGE HEADING.  THEN THE INPUT IS LISTED AND PARSED  */00000126
   127    /*    INPUT CONSISTS OF SECTIONS AND COMMAND.  EACH SECTION STARTS   */00000127
   128    /*    WITH '.NAME ' IN COL 1.  VALID NAMES ARE LISTED BELOW.         */00000128
   129    /*    COMMAND START WITH '.KW=' IN COL 1.                            */00000129
   130    /*                                                                   */00000130
   131    /* THERE ARE 3 SECTIONS                                              */00000131
   132    /* 1.  ATTR - THIS IS WHERE THE ATTRIBUTES ARE DEFINED. THESE MUST   */00000132
   133    /*     BE DEFINED BEFORE USE IN THE SCREEN SECTION.                  */00000133
   134    /* 2.  SCREEN - THIS IS WHERE THE 'DRAWING' OF THE SCREEN IS         */00000134
   135    /*     IS DEFINED.  EACH FIELD BEGIN WITH AN ATTRIBUTED AS DEFINED   */00000135
   136    /*     IN THE ATTR SECTION.                                          */00000136
   137    /* 3.  VARS - THIS OPTIONAL SECTION MAPS ANY USER DEFINED FIELD      */00000137
   138    /*     NAME TO BE DEFINED.  THESE NAME REPLACE THE DEFAULT NAME OF   */00000138
   139    /*     R99C99.                                                       */00000139
   140    /*                                                                   */00000140
   141    /* THE FOLLOWING IS A LIST OF COMMAND CURRENTLY SUPPORTED:           */00000141
   142    /*                                                                   */00000142
   143    /* 1.  .NAME= THIS COMMAND SETS THE NAME FOR THE PANEL.  NAME CAN    */00000143
   144    /*     BE ANY VALID NAME 1-7 CHARACTERS.  MAP3270 GENERATES SOME     */00000144
   145    /*     INTERNAL NAMES USING 'NAME' PLUS 1 CHARACTER.                 */00000145
   146    /*                                                                   */00000146
   147    /*********************************************************************/00000147
   148                                                                           00000148
   149       DT_TIME_STAMP = '** GENERATED BY MAP3270 V2.1.0 ON ' ||             00000149
   150                       DATE || ' AT ' || TIME;                             00000150
   151       TITLE_STAMP = ' GENERATED BY MAP3270 V2.1.0';                       00000151
   152       CALL INITIALIZE;                                                    00000152
   153       ON ENDPAGE(SYSPRINT)                                                00000153
   154       BEGIN;                                                              00000154
   155          PAGE_NO = PAGE_NO + 1;                                           00000155
   156          PUT PAGE EDIT(PAGE_TITLE,PGM_VER,'PAGE ',PAGE_NO)                00000156
   157                       (A,COL(100),A,COL(111),A,F(3));                     00000157
   158          PUT SKIP(2) EDIT('INPUT STATEMENTS')(A)                          00000158
   159                          (' LINE:   STATEMENT') (SKIP(2),A)               00000159
   160                          ('------   ---------') (SKIP,A);                 00000160
   161       END;                                                                00000161
   162                                                                           00000162
   163       SIGNAL ENDPAGE(SYSPRINT);                                           00000163
   164       PROCESS_STATUS = '.NONE';                                           00000164
   165       ON ENDFILE(SYSIN)                                                   00000165
   166          NOT_E_O_F = FALSE;                                               00000166
   167       NOT_E_O_F = TRUE;                                                   00000167

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE      9


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   168    /*********************************************************************/00000168
   169    /*                                                                   */00000169
   170    /*  PPPP    AAA    SSS    SSS     1                                  */00000170
   171    /*  P   P  A   A  S      S       11                                  */00000171
   172    /*  PPPP   A   A  S      S        1                                  */00000172
   173    /*  P      AAAAA   SSS    SSS     1                                  */00000173
   174    /*  P      A   A      S      S    1                                  */00000174
   175    /*  P      A   A      S      S    1                                  */00000175
   176    /*  P      A   A   SSS    SSS   11111                                */00000176
   177    /*                                                                   */00000177
   178    /*  READ AND PRINT THE INPUT STATEMENTS                              */00000178
   179    /*    DETERMINE THE SECTION AND PASS TO THE APPROPRIATE SECTION      */00000179
   180    /*    FOR PROCESSING.                                                */00000180
   181    /*    COMMANDS ARE PARSED AND PROCESSED IMMEDIATELY.                 */00000181
   182    /*                                                                   */00000182
   183    /*********************************************************************/00000183
   184       GET EDIT(MY_REC) (A(80));                                           00000184
   185       DO WHILE (NOT_E_O_F);                                               00000185
   186          REC_CTR = REC_CTR + 1;                                           00000186
   187          PUT SKIP EDIT(REC_CTR,':',MY_REC) (F(5),A(4),A);                 00000187
   188          IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,5) = '.ATTR' THEN                             00000188
   189          DO;                                                              00000189
   190               PROCESS_STATUS = '.ATTR  ';                                 00000190
   191               A = 0;                                                      00000191
   192               ATTRLIST='';                                                00000192
   193          END;                                                             00000193
   194          ELSE                                                             00000194
   195          IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,7) = '.SCREEN' THEN                           00000195
   196          DO;                                                              00000196
   197               PROCESS_STATUS = '.SCREEN';                                 00000197
   198               B = 0;                                                      00000198
   199               FLD_DEF = '';                                               00000199
   200               FLD_A = 0;                                                  00000200
   201               ROW = 0;                                                    00000201
   202               COL = 0;                                                    00000202
   203               NO_ATTRIB = TRUE;                                           00000203
   204          END;                                                             00000204
   205          ELSE                                                             00000205
   206          IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,5) = '.VARS' THEN                             00000206
   207               PROCESS_STATUS = '.VARS  ';                                 00000207
   208          ELSE                                                             00000208
   209          IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6) = '.NAME=' THEN                            00000209
   210          BEGIN;                                                           00000210
   211               DCL I FIXED BINARY(15);                                     00000211
   212               PANEL_NAME = SUBSTR(MY_REC,7,7);                            00000212

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     10


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   213               I = INDEX(PANEL_NAME,' ');                                  00000213
   214               IF I > 0 THEN PANEL_NAME=SUBSTR(PANEL_NAME,1,I-1);          00000214
   215          END;                                                             00000215
   216          ELSE                                                             00000216
   217          IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,1) = '*' THEN; /* DO NOT PROCESS COMMENT */   00000217
   218          ELSE                                                             00000218
   219               CALL PROCESS_MYREC;                                         00000219
   220          GET EDIT(MY_REC) (A(80));                                        00000220
   221       END; /* OF LOOP */                                                  00000221
   222       IF FLD_DEF ^= '' THEN             /* IF WE STILL HAVE DATA      */  00000222
   223       DO;                                                                 00000223
   224          CALL SAVE_FIELD(ONE);          /* WRITE DATA FOR LAST FIELD  */  00000224
   225          FLD_DEF = '';                                                    00000225
   226       END;                                                                00000226

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     11



   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   227    /*********************************************************************/00000227
   228    /*                                                                   */00000228
   229    /*  PPPP    AAA    SSS    SSS    222                                 */00000229
   230    /*  P   P  A   A  S      S      2   2                                */00000230
   231    /*  PPPP   A   A  S      S          2                                */00000231
   232    /*  P      AAAAA   SSS    SSS      2                                 */00000232
   233    /*  P      A   A      S      S    2                                  */00000233
   234    /*  P      A   A      S      S   2                                   */00000234
   235    /*  P      A   A   SSS    SSS   22222                                */00000235
   236    /*                                                                   */00000236
   237    /*  SET UP THE PAGE HEADINGS FOR THE SECOND PASS.                    */00000237
   238    /*    DURING THE SECOND PASS, SOME ERROR CHECKING IS PERFORMED TO    */00000238
   239    /*    ENSURE THE MAP DOES NOT VIOLATE HARDWARE PROTOCOL.             */00000239
   240    /*                                                                   */00000240
   241    /*   -THE SCREEN IMAGE WILL BE PRINTED.                              */00000241
   242    /*   -THE INPUT ATTRIBUTES AND THE GENERATED ATTRIBUTES WILL BE      */00000242
   243    /*    PRINTED.  THIS SHOWS WHAT WAS SPECIFIED VS WHAT WILL BE        */00000243
   244    /*    GENERATED.                                                     */00000244
   245    /*   -ALL VARIABLE NAMES ARE CORRECT AND EXIST                       */00000245
   246    /*   -THE MACROS TO DEFINE THE PHYSICAL MAP (NOT RELATED TO CICS)    */00000246
   247    /*   -THE USER INTERFACE(S) FOR ASSEMBLER, COBOL AND PL1 PROGRAMS.   */00000247
   248    /*                                                                   */00000248
   249    /*********************************************************************/00000249
   250                                                                           00000250
   251       ON ENDPAGE(SYSPRINT)                                                00000251
   252       BEGIN;                                                              00000252
   253          PAGE_NO = PAGE_NO + 1;                                           00000253
   254          PUT PAGE EDIT(PAGE_TITLE,'PANEL ',PANEL_NAME,                    00000254
   255                        PGM_VER,'PAGE ',PAGE_NO)                           00000255
   256                       (A,COL(70),A,A,COL(100),A,COL(111),A,F(3));         00000256
   257          PUT SKIP(2);                                                     00000257
   258       END;                                                                00000258
   259       SIGNAL ENDPAGE(SYSPRINT);                                           00000259
   260                                                                           00000260
   261          /*  PRINT THE SCREEN IMAGE */                                    00000261
   262                                                                           00000262
   263       PUT SKIP EDIT('* ', (29)'>',                                        00000263
   264                     ' SAMPLE SCREEN LAYOUT ',                             00000264
   265                     (29)'<') (X(10),(4)A);                                00000265
   266       PUT SKIP EDIT('*') (X(10),A);                                       00000266
   267       PUT SKIP EDIT('* ----+----1----+----2----+----3',                   00000267
   268                       '----+----4----+----5----+----6',                   00000268
   269                       '----+----7----+----8') (X(10),(3)A);               00000269
   270       DO I = 1 TO B;                                                      00000270
   271          PUT SKIP EDIT(I,SCR_IMG(I)) (F(9),X(1),A);                       00000271

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     12


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   272       END;                                                                00000272
   273       PUT SKIP EDIT('* ----+----1----+----2----+----3',                   00000273
   274                       '----+----4----+----5----+----6',                   00000274
   275                       '----+----7----+----8') (X(10),(3)A);               00000275
   276                                                                           00000276
   277          /*  PRINT THE ATTRIBUTE LIST */                                  00000277
   278                                                                           00000278
   279       PUT SKIP(2) EDIT('CHAR ATTR')(X(10),A);                             00000279
   280       DO I = 1 TO A;                                                      00000280
   281          PUT SKIP EDIT(ATTR_TBL(I).ATTR_CHR,                              00000281
   282                        ATTR_TBL(I).ATTR_A) (X(12),A,X(2),A);              00000282
   283          PUT SKIP EDIT(' ') (X(15),A);                                    00000283
   284          CALL PRINT_ATTR(ATTR_TBL(I));                                    00000284
   285       END; /* OF LOOP */                                                  00000285
   286                                                                           00000286
   287          /*  VERIFY THE FIELDS LIST  */                                   00000287
   288                                                                           00000288
   289       DECLARE VAR_FLD_MATCH  BIT(1) ALIGNED;                              00000289
   290       DO I=1 TO VAR_CTR;                                                  00000290
   291         VAR_FLD_MATCH = FALSE;                                            00000291
   292         DO J=1 TO FLD_CTR;                                                00000292
   293            IF VAR(I).VAR_NAME = FLD(J).FLD_NAME THEN                      00000293

   296           /** IF ATTR_TBL(FLD(J).FLD_ATTR).TITLE THEN                     00000296
   297               DO;                                                         00000297
   298                  PUT SKIP EDIT('*** VAR ',VAR(I).VAR_NAME,                00000298
   299                                ' IS LISTED IN THE .VAR SECTION. THE ',    00000299
   300                                'FIELD IS A TITLE. NAME NOT ALLOWED.')     00000300
   301                                (A,A,A,A);                                 00000301
   302                  ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                      00000302
   303               END;                                                        00000303
   304               ELSE                                                        00000304
   305           **/    FLD(J).FLD_NAME = VAR(I).VAR_FLD;                        00000305
   306            END;                                                           00000306
   307         END;                                                              00000307
   308         IF VAR_FLD_MATCH  THEN ;                                          00000308
   309         ELSE                                                              00000309
   310         DO;                                                               00000310
   311            PUT SKIP EDIT('*** VAR ',VAR(I).VAR_NAME,' IS LISTED IN THE',  00000311
   312                          ' .VAR SECTION BUT IS NOT DEFINED ***')          00000312
   313                         (A,A,A,A);                                        00000313
   314            ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                            00000314
   315         END;                                                              00000315
   316       END;                                                                00000316

   317                                                                           00000317
   318          /*  PRINT THE FIELDS LIST  */                                    00000318
