           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     15


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   385    /*********************************************************************/00000385
   386    /*                                                                   */00000386
   387    /*   THIS IS THE MAIN INPUT PROCESS CONTROL.  NOTE THAT THERE IS     */00000387
   388    /*   NO ENFORCMENT OF THE SEQUENCE OF THE INPUT SECTIONS.            */00000388
   389    /*   THE CORRECT SEQUENCE IS .ATTR, .SCREEN, .VARS                   */00000389
   390    /*                                                                   */00000390
   391    /*********************************************************************/00000391

   392    PROCESS_MYREC:PROC;                                                    00000392
   393                                                                           00000393
   394      IF PROCESS_STATUS = '.ATTR  '        THEN CALL PROCESS_ATTRIBUTE;    00000394
   395      ELSE IF  PROCESS_STATUS = '.SCREEN'  THEN CALL PROCESS_SCREEN;       00000395
   396      ELSE IF  PROCESS_STATUS = '.VARS  '  THEN CALL PROCESS_VARS;         00000396
   397                                                                           00000397
   398    END PROCESS_MYREC;                                                     00000398
   399                                                                           00000399
   400    PROCESS_ATTRIBUTE:PROC;                                                00000400
   401       DECLARE ATTRIB              CHAR(1);                                00000401
   402       DECLARE (TEMP,TEMP2)        CHAR(78) VARYING;                       00000402
   403       DECLARE I                   FIXED BINARY(15);                       00000403
   404       I = 3;                                                              00000404
   405       DO WHILE (I<80 & SUBSTR(MY_REC,I,1)^=' ');                          00000405
   406          I=I+1;                                                           00000406
   407       END;                                                                00000407
   408       TEMP,TEMP2 = SUBSTR(MY_REC,3,I-3);                                  00000408
   409       A = A + 1;                                                          00000409
   410       ATTR_TBL(A).ATTR_A = '('||TEMP2||')';                               00000410
   411       ATTR_TBL(A).ATTR_CHR = SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,1);                          00000411
   412       I=1;                                                                00000412
   413       DO WHILE(I>0);                                                      00000413
   414          I=INDEX(TEMP,',');                                               00000414
   415          IF I>0 THEN                                                      00000415
   416          DO;                                                              00000416
   417             CALL CHECK_ATTR(SUBSTR(TEMP,1,I-1),ATTR_TBL(A));              00000417
   418             TEMP=SUBSTR(TEMP,I+1);                                        00000418
   419          END;                                                             00000419
   420          ELSE                                                             00000420
   421             CALL CHECK_ATTR(TEMP,ATTR_TBL(A));                            00000421
   422       END;                                                                00000422
   423       IF ATTR_TBL(A).TITLE THEN          /* OVERRIDE SOME ATTRS  */       00000423
   424       DO;                                /* FOR TYPE TITLE       */       00000424
   425          ATTR_TBL(A).TITLE = TRUE;                                        00000425
   426          ATTR_TBL(A).PROT = TRUE;                                         00000426
   427       /**ATTR_TBL(A).BRIGHT = FALSE;  DO NOT OVERRIDE BRIGHT   **/        00000427
   428          ATTR_TBL(A).NUM = FALSE;                                         00000428

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     16


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   429          ATTR_TBL(A).STOP_BIT = FALSE;                                    00000429
   430          ATTR_TBL(A).CUR = FALSE;                                         00000430
   431       END;                                                                00000431
   432     /*PUT SKIP DATA(A,ATTR_TBL(A));*/                                     00000432
   433    END PROCESS_ATTRIBUTE;                                                 00000433

   434    /*********************************************************************/00000434
   435    /*                                                                   */00000435
   436    /*   THIS ROUTINE PROCESSES ALL OF THE ATTRIBUTES.  THEY CAN BE      */00000436
   437    /*   SPECIFIED IN THE .ATTR OR .VARS SECTION.  THE MAP DEFAULTS      */00000437
   438    /*   CAN BE SET IN THE .ATTR AND OVERRIDEN FOR EACH FIELD IN THE     */00000438
   439    /*   .VARS SECTION.                                                  */00000439
   440    /*                                                                   */00000440
   441    /*********************************************************************/00000441

   442    CHECK_ATTR:PROC(AT,ATTR);                                              00000442
   443       DCL AT CHAR(*) VARYING,                                             00000443
   444           ATTR LIKE ATTR_REC;                                             00000444
   445       SELECT (AT);                                                        00000445
   446         WHEN ('TITLE')     ATTR.TITLE = TRUE;                             00000446
   447         WHEN ('BRIGHT')    ATTR.BRIGHT = TRUE;                            00000447
   448         WHEN ('NORMAL')    ATTR.BRIGHT = FALSE;                           00000448
   449         WHEN ('NUM')       ATTR.NUM = TRUE;                               00000449
   450         WHEN ('ALPHA')     ATTR.NUM = FALSE;                              00000450
   451         WHEN ('PROT')      ATTR.PROT = TRUE;                              00000451
   452         WHEN ('UNPROT')    ATTR.PROT = FALSE;                             00000452
   453         WHEN ('CUR')       ATTR.CUR = TRUE;                               00000453
   454         WHEN ('STOP')      ATTR.STOP_BIT = TRUE;                          00000454
   455         WHEN ('HIDEF')     ATTR.HI_LIGHT = 'D';                           00000455
   456         WHEN ('BLINK')     ATTR.HI_LIGHT = 'B';                           00000456
   457         WHEN ('REVERSE')   ATTR.HI_LIGHT = 'R';                           00000457
   458         WHEN ('ULINE')     ATTR.HI_LIGHT = 'U';                           00000458
   459                                              /* COLOR CODE */             00000459
   460         WHEN ('DEFAULT')   ATTR.COLOR = 'DEF';  /* 40 */                  00000460
   461         WHEN ('BLUE')      ATTR.COLOR = 'BLU';  /* F1 */                  00000461
   462         WHEN ('RED')       ATTR.COLOR = 'RED';  /* F2 */                  00000462
   463         WHEN ('PINK')      ATTR.COLOR = 'PNK';  /* F3 */                  00000463
   464         WHEN ('GREEN')     ATTR.COLOR = 'GRN';  /* F4 */                  00000464
   465         WHEN ('TURQ')      ATTR.COLOR = 'TUR';  /* F5 */                  00000465
   466         WHEN ('YELLOW')    ATTR.COLOR = 'YEL';  /* F6 */                  00000466
   467         WHEN ('WHITE')     ATTR.COLOR = 'WHI';  /* F7 */                  00000467
   468         WHEN ('BLACK')     ATTR.COLOR = 'BLK';  /* F8 */                  00000468
   469         WHEN ('DBLUE')     ATTR.COLOR = 'DBL';  /* F9 */                  00000469
   470         WHEN ('ORANGE')    ATTR.COLOR = 'ORA';  /* FA */                  00000470
   471         WHEN ('PURPLE')    ATTR.COLOR = 'PUR';  /* FB */                  00000471

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     17


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   472         WHEN ('PGREEN')    ATTR.COLOR = 'PGR';  /* FC */                  00000472
   473         WHEN ('PTURQ')     ATTR.COLOR = 'PTQ';  /* FD */                  00000473
   474         WHEN ('GREY')      ATTR.COLOR = 'GRY';  /* FE */                  00000474
   475         WHEN ('NEUTRAL')   ATTR.COLOR = 'NEU';  /* FF */                  00000475
   476       OTHERWISE                                                           00000476
   477       DO;                                                                 00000477
   478          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** INVALID ATTRIBUTE ''',AT,''' DETECTED ***')   00000478
   479                       (A,A,A);                                            00000479
   480          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                              00000480
   481       END;                                                                00000481
   482     /*PUT SKIP LIST(ATTR.COLOR);*/                                        00000482
   483    END CHECK_ATTR;                                                        00000483

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     18


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   484    /*********************************************************************/00000484
   485    /*                                                                   */00000485
   486    /*   THIS ROUTINE PROCESSES ALL OF THE VARS LINES.  THE GENERAL      */00000486
   487    /*   FORMAT IS:                                                      */00000487
   488    /*   R99C99=NAME123,ATTR,ATTR COMMENTS                               */00000488
   489    /*   R99C99 IS THE NAME GENERATED BY MAP3270.                        */00000489
   490    /*   NAME IS 1 TO 7 CHARACTER NAME ASSIGNED BY THE PROGRAMMER.       */00000490
   491    /*   ,ATTR IS AN ADDITIONAL OR OVERRIDE ATTRIBUTE FOR THIS FIELD.    */00000491
   492    /*         0 OR MORE ATTRS MAY BE SPECIFIED.  THE LIST ENDS WHEN     */00000492
   493    /*         THE FIRST SPACE IS ENCOUNTERED.                           */00000493
   494    /*                                                                   */00000494
   495    /*********************************************************************/00000495
   496                                                                           00000496
   497    PROCESS_VARS:PROC;                                                     00000497
   498       DECLARE (MATCH_INI_NAME,MATCH_NAME) BIT(1) ALIGNED;                 00000498
   499       DECLARE (TEMP,TEMP2)        CHAR(78) VARYING;                       00000499
   500       DECLARE (I,COMMA,BLANK,NST,NLEN) FIXED BINARY(15) ALIGNED;          00000500
   501       DECLARE (FLD_NAME_PTR)           FIXED BINARY(15) ALIGNED;          00000501
   502       IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,7,1)^='=' THEN                                     00000502
   503       DO;                                                                 00000503
   504          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** EXPECTED ''='' NOT FOUND ***') (A);           00000504
   505          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                              00000505
   506          RETURN;                                                          00000506
   507       END;                                                                00000507
   508       COMMA=INDEX(MY_REC,',');                                            00000508
   509       BLANK=INDEX(MY_REC,' ');                                            00000509
   510       NST=8;                                                              00000510
   511       SELECT (TRUE);                                                      00000511
   512          WHEN (COMMA=0 & BLANK>0)  /* NO COMMA FOUND BUT A BLANK WAS */   00000512
   513              NLEN=BLANK-NST;                                              00000513
   514          WHEN (BLANK=0 & COMMA>0)    /* NO BLANK FOUND BUT A COMMA WAS */ 00000514
   515              NLEN=COMMA-NST;                                              00000515
   516          WHEN (COMMA<BLANK)    /* ATTR STARTS BEFORE BLANK       */       00000516
   517              NLEN=COMMA-NST;                                              00000517
   518          WHEN (COMMA>BLANK)    /* BLANK APPEARS BEFORE COMMA     */       00000518
   519              NLEN=BLANK-NST;                                              00000519
   520          OTHERWISE                                                        00000520
   521          DO;                                                              00000521
   522             PUT SKIP EDIT('*** LOGIC ERROR 1 ***') (A);                   00000522
   523             ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                           00000523
   524             RETURN;                                                       00000524
   525          END;                                                             00000525
   526       IF NLEN>7 THEN                                                      00000526
   527       DO;                                                                 00000527
   528          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** INCORRECT FIELD LENGTHS ***') (A);            00000528

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     19


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   529          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                              00000529
   530          RETURN;                                                          00000530
   531       END;                                                                00000531
   532       DO I = 1 TO VAR_CTR;                                                00000532
   533          IF VAR(I).VAR_NAME = SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6) THEN                     00000533
   534          DO;                                                              00000534
   535              PUT SKIP EDIT('*** DUPLICATE VAR NAME ',VAR(I).VAR_NAME,     00000535
   536                           ' ***') (A,A,A);                                00000536
   537              ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                          00000537
   538              RETURN;                                                      00000538
   539          END;                                                             00000539
   540          IF VAR(I).VAR_FLD = SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST,NLEN) THEN                 00000540
   541          DO;                                                              00000541
   542              PUT SKIP EDIT('*** DUPLICATE VAR FIELD ',                    00000542
   543                            SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST,NLEN),' ***') (A,A,A);       00000543
   544              ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                          00000544
   545              RETURN;                                                      00000545
   546          END;                                                             00000546
   547       END;                                                                00000547
   548       MATCH_INI_NAME=FALSE;                                               00000548
   549       MATCH_NAME=FALSE;                                                   00000549
   550       FLD_NAME_PTR=0;                                                     00000550
   551       DO WHILE(FLD_NAME_PTR<FLD_CTR & ^MATCH_INI_NAME);                   00000551
   552          FLD_NAME_PTR=FLD_NAME_PTR+1;                                     00000552
   553          MATCH_INI_NAME =                                                 00000553
   554                (FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).FLD_INT_NAME = SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6));     00000554
   555       END;                                                                00000555
   556       IF MATCH_INI_NAME THEN ;                                            00000556
   557       ELSE                                                                00000557
   558       DO;                                                                 00000558
   559          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** INTERNAL NAME NOT DEFINED ',                  00000559
   560                        SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6),                                00000560
   561                        ' ***') (A,A,A);                                   00000561
   562          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                              00000562
   563          RETURN;                                                          00000563
   564       END;                                                                00000564
   565       VAR_CTR=VAR_CTR+1;                                                  00000565
   566       VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_NAME=SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6);                           00000566
   567       VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_FLD=SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST,NLEN);                       00000567
   568       I=INDEX(VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_FLD,' ');                                  00000568
   569       IF I=0 THEN ;               /* NAME HAS NO SPACES - IT IS OK */     00000569
   570       ELSE                                                                00000570
   571       IF I=1 THEN                                                         00000571
   572       DO;                                                                 00000572
   573          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** USER DEFINED NAME IS BLANK ***') (A);         00000573

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     20


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   574          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                              00000574
   575          RETURN;                                                          00000575
   576       END;                                                                00000576
   577       IF COMMA=0 | BLANK<COMMA THEN    /* NO ATTRIBUTES */                00000577
   578           RETURN;                                                         00000578
   579       TEMP,TEMP2 = SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST+NLEN+1);  /* GET RID OF NAME */      00000579
   580       BLANK=INDEX(TEMP,' ');                                              00000580
   581       IF BLANK>0 THEN TEMP,TEMP2=SUBSTR(TEMP,1,BLANK-1);                  00000581
   582       FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).ATTR_A=FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).ATTR_A||'<'||TEMP2||'>'; 00000582
   583       I=1;                                                                00000583
   584       DO WHILE(I>0);                                                      00000584
   585          I=INDEX(TEMP,',');                                               00000585
   586          IF I>0 THEN                                                      00000586
   587          DO;                                                              00000587
   588             CALL CHECK_ATTR(SUBSTR(TEMP,1,I-1),FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).FLD_REC);00000588
   589             TEMP=SUBSTR(TEMP,I+1);                                        00000589
   590          END;                                                             00000590
   591          ELSE                                                             00000591
   592             CALL CHECK_ATTR(TEMP,FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).FLD_REC);              00000592
   593       END;                                                                00000593
   594    /* PUT SKIP LIST ('INPUT=>',VAR_CTR,VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_NAME,             00000594
   595                                  ''''||VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_FLD||'''');       00000595
   596       PUT SKIP DATA (FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR)); */                               00000596
   597    END PROCESS_VARS;                                                      00000597

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     21


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   598    /****************************************************************/     00000598
   599    PROCESS_SCREEN:PROC;                                                   00000599
   600                                                                           00000600
   601       DECLARE (C,I               ) FIXED BINARY(15),                      00000601
   602                K                   CHAR(1);                               00000602
   603       NO_ATTRIB = TRUE;                                                   00000603
   604       ROW = ROW + 1;                               /* COUNT ROW WE ARE  */00000604
   605       B = B + 1; SCR_IMG(B) = '* ' || MY_REC;                             00000605
   606       COL = 1;                                                            00000606
   607       FLD_A = 1;                                                          00000607
   608       DO C = 1 TO 80;                              /* PROCESS ONE BY ONE*/00000608
   609          K = SUBSTR(MY_REC,C,1);                   /* GET NEXT BYTE     */00000609
   610          DO I = 1 TO A;                            /* TEST IF ATTRIBUTE */00000610
   611             IF ATTR_TBL(I).ATTR_CHR = K THEN       /* IF WE FIND AN     */00000611
   612             DO;                                    /*  ATTRIBUTE        */00000612
   613                NO_ATTRIB = FALSE;                                         00000613
   614                IF FLD_DEF  ^= '' THEN              /* AND WE ALREADY    */00000614
   615                DO;                                                        00000615
   616                    CALL SAVE_FIELD(FLD_A);         /*  HAVE DATA        */00000616
   617                    FLD_DEF = '';                                          00000617
   618                END;                                                       00000618
   619                COL = C;                                                   00000619
   620                FLD_A = I;                                                 00000620
   621             END; /* IF */                                                 00000621
   622          END; /* DO */                                                    00000622
   623       /* IF NO_ATTRIB THEN  ;                                             00000623
   624          ELSE                                                             00000624
   625       */ DO;                                                              00000625
   626             FLD_DEF = FLD_DEF  || K;                                      00000626
   627            /*  IF SUBSTR(X,C,1)= '''' THEN DATA = DATA  ''''  */        00000627
   628          END;                                                             00000628
   629       END; /* DO */                                                       00000629
   630       IF LENGTH(FLD_DEF)>0 THEN                                           00000630
   631       DO;                                                                 00000631
   632          CALL SAVE_FIELD(FLD_A);                                          00000632
   633          FLD_DEF = '';                                                    00000633
   634       END;                                                                00000634
   635    END PROCESS_SCREEN;                                                    00000635

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     22


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   636    /****************************************************************/     00000636
   637    SAVE_FIELD:PROC(I);                                                    00000637
   638       DECLARE I FIXED BINARY(15);                                         00000638
   639       DECLARE (R,C) PICTURE '99';                                         00000639
   640       FLD_CTR = FLD_CTR + 1;                                              00000640
   641       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_DATA = FLD_DEF;                                    00000641
   642       R=ROW;                                                              00000642
   643       C=COL;                                                              00000643
   644       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_INT_NAME,                                          00000644
   645       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_NAME = 'R'||R||'C'||C;                             00000645
   646       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_ROW  = ROW;                                        00000646
   647       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_COL  = COL;                                        00000647
   648       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_ATTR = I;                                          00000648
   649       FLD(FLD_CTR).FLD_REC = ATTR_TBL(I);                                 00000649
   650     /*PUT SKIP DATA(FLD(FLD_CTR));*/                                      00000650
   651    END SAVE_FIELD;                                                        00000651

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     23


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   652    /*********************************************************************/00000652
   653    /*                                                                   */00000653
   654    /* PRINT_ATTR - PRINT ATTRIBUTES FOR A GIVEN FIELD                   */00000654
   655    /*                                                                   */00000655
   656    /*********************************************************************/00000656
   657    PRINT_ATTR:PROC(ATTR);                                                 00000657
   658       DECLARE ATTR LIKE ATTR_REC;                                         00000658
   659          IF ATTR.TITLE THEN                                               00000659
   660             PUT EDIT('TITLE ') (A);                                       00000660
   661                                                                           00000661
   662          IF ATTR.NUM THEN PUT EDIT('NUM ') (A);                           00000662
   663          ELSE PUT EDIT('ALPHA ') (A);                                     00000663
   664                                                                           00000664
   665          IF ATTR.PROT THEN PUT EDIT('PROT ') (A);                         00000665
   666          ELSE PUT EDIT('UNPROT ') (A);                                    00000666
   667                                                                           00000667
   668          IF ATTR.BRIGHT THEN PUT EDIT('BRIGHT ') (A);                     00000668
   669          ELSE PUT EDIT('NORMAL ') (A);                                    00000669
   670                                                                           00000670
   671          SELECT (ATTR.HI_LIGHT)                                           00000671
   672              WHEN (' ')  ;                                                00000672
   673              WHEN ('D')  PUT EDIT('HI DEFAULT ') (A);                     00000673
   674              WHEN ('U')  PUT EDIT('UNDERLINE ') (A);                      00000674
   675              WHEN ('R')  PUT EDIT('REVERSE ') (A);                        00000675
   676              WHEN ('B')  PUT EDIT('BLINK ') (A);                          00000676
   677              OTHERWISE                                                    00000677
   678              DO;                                                          00000678
   679                  PUT SKIP(2) EDIT('*** ERROR *** INVALID ATTRIBUTE ',     00000679
   680                                   'VALUE ***') (A,A);                     00000680
   681                  ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                      00000681
   682              END;                                                         00000682
   683                                                                           00000683
   684          IF ATTR.CUR  THEN PUT EDIT('CUR ') (A);                          00000684
   685                                                                           00000685
   686          IF ATTR.STOP_BIT THEN PUT EDIT('STOP ') (A);                     00000686
   687          PUT EDIT(ATTR.COLOR,' ') (A,A);                                  00000687
   688    END PRINT_ATTR;                                                        00000688

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     24


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   689    /*********************************************************************/00000689
   690    /*                                                                   */00000690
   691    /* WRITE_PANEL - WRITE THE MACROS TO GENERATE THE PANEL              */00000691
   692    /*                                                                   */00000692
   693    /* IN THE MAP3270 SYSTEM, THE PANEL IS A LOAD MODULE GENERATED FROM  */00000693
   694    /* ASSEMBLER CODE GENERATED BY THIS PROGRAM.  THE PANEL HAS 3        */00000694
   695    /* SECTIONS:                                                         */00000695
   696    /*    1) INDEX TO THE  DATA STREAM, CROSS REFERENCE AND INSERT       */00000696
   697    /*       CURSOR AREAS.                                               */00000697
   698    /*    2) 3270 DATA STEAM WHICH CONTAINS THE INSERT CURSOR STUFF.     */00000698
   699    /*    3) CROSS REFERENCE WHICH MAPS THE FIELDS IN THE DATA STREAM    */00000699
   700    /*       TO THE USER MAP.                                            */00000700
   701    /*                                                                   */00000701
   702    /*********************************************************************/00000702
   703    WRITE_PANEL:PROC;                                                      00000703
   704       DECLARE M FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000704
   705       DECLARE IC_WRITTEN  BIT(1) ALIGNED;                                 00000705
   706                                                                           00000706
   707       OPEN FILE(PANEL) TITLE('MAP');                                      00000707
   708                                                                           00000708
   709       PUT FILE(PANEL) EDIT('TITLE ''PANEL ',PANEL_NAME,' ',               00000709
   710                            TITLE_STAMP,'''')     (COL(10),A,A,A,A,A)      00000710
   711                           (PANEL_SEQ)            (COL(73),P'999999V99');  00000711
   712       PANE_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                               00000712
   713       PUT FILE(PANEL) EDIT(DT_TIME_STAMP)                    (COL(1),A)   00000713
   714                           (PANEL_SEQ)            (COL(73),P'999999V99')   00000714
   715                           (PANEL_NAME,'TSECT')            (A,COL(10),A)   00000715
   716                           (PANEL_SEQ+1)          (COL(73),P'999999V99')   00000716
   717                           ('DC    A(', PANEL_NAME||'P)' ) (COL(10),A,A)   00000717
   718                           (PANEL_SEQ+2)          (COL(73),P'999999V99')   00000718
   719                           ('DC    A(', PANEL_NAME||'M)' ) (COL(10),A,A)   00000719
   720                           (PANEL_SEQ+3)          (COL(73),P'999999V99')   00000720
   721                           ('DC    A(', PANEL_NAME||'C)' ) (COL(10),A,A)   00000721
   722                           (PANEL_SEQ+4)          (COL(73),P'999999V99');  00000722
   723       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+5;                                              00000723
   724       PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                     00000724
   725                  EDIT(PANEL_NAME,'TSTPAN',PANEL_SEQ)                      00000725
   726                                       (A,COL(10),A,COL(73),P'999999V99')  00000726
   727                      ('TWCC  RESET=YES,RSTMDT=YES',PANEL_SEQ+1)           00000727
   728                                         (COL(10),A,COL(73),P'999999V99'); 00000728
   729       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+2;                                              00000729
   730       IC_WRITTEN=FALSE;                                                   00000730
   731       M = FLD_CTR;                                                        00000731
   732       DO WHILE (M>0);                                                     00000732
   733          IF ATTR_TBL(FLD(M).FLD_ATTR).CUR THEN                            00000733

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     25


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   734          DO;                                                              00000734
   735             CALL WRITE_IC(FLD(M).FLD_ROW,FLD(M).FLD_COL);                 00000735
   736             IC_WRITTEN=TRUE;                                              00000736
   737             M = 0;                                                        00000737
   738          END;                                                             00000738
   739          M=M-1;                                                           00000739
   740       END;  /* DO */                                                      00000740
   741       IF ^IC_WRITTEN THEN                                                 00000741
   742          CALL WRITE_IC(ONE,ONE);                                          00000742
   743       DO M = 1 TO FLD_CTR;                                                00000743
   744          CALL WRITE_FIELD(M);                                             00000744
   745       END;                                                                00000745
   746       PUT FILE(PANEL) EDIT('TENDPAN',PANEL_SEQ)                           00000746
   747                                       (COL(10),A,COL(73),P'999999V99');   00000747
   748       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                              00000748
   749    /****************************************************************/     00000749
   750    WRITE_IC:PROC(R,C);                                                    00000750
   751       DECLARE (R,C)  FIXED BIN(15);                                       00000751
   752                                                                           00000752
   753       PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                     00000753
   754                EDIT(PANEL_NAME||'C',                                      00000754
   755                            'TCMD  CMD=SBA,ROW=',R,',COL=',C,PANEL_SEQ)    00000755
   756                         (A,COL(10),A,P'99',A,P'99',COL(73),P'999999V99')  00000756
   757                    ('         TCMD  CMD=IC',PANEL_SEQ+1)                  00000757
   758                                                (A,COL(73),P'999999V99');  00000758
   759       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+2;                                              00000759
   760                                                                           00000760
   761    END WRITE_IC;                                                          00000761
   762    /****************************************************************/     00000762
   763    WRITE_FIELD:PROC(F);                                                   00000763
   764       DECLARE F FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000764
   765       DECLARE A FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000765
   766       DECLARE I FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000766
   767       DECLARE MACRO_LN CHAR(160) VARYING;                                 00000767
   768       DECLARE LN_PIC   PIC '99';                                          00000768
   769       DECLARE FLD_NAME CHAR(8) VARYING;   /* FORMAT R99C99 */             00000769
   770       A = FLD(F).FLD_ATTR;                                                00000770
   771     /*****                                                                00000771
   772       PUT SKIP DATA(FLD(F));                                              00000772
   773       PUT SKIP DATA(ATTR_TBL(A));                                         00000773
   774     *****/                                                                00000774
   775       FLD_DEF=SUBSTR(FLD(F).FLD_DATA,2);                                  00000775
   776       I = LENGTH(FLD_DEF);                                                00000776
   777       DO WHILE(SUBSTR(FLD_DEF,I,1)=' ' & I>0);                            00000777
   778          I=I-1;                                                           00000778

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     26


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   779       END;                                                                00000779
   780       IF I=0 THEN FLD_DEF='';                                             00000780
   781       ELSE FLD_DEF=SUBSTR(FLD_DEF,1,I);                                   00000781
   782    /* PUT SKIP DATA(FLD_DEF); */                                          00000782
   783       /* MAKE SURE THAT FIELDS DON'T GO PAST COL 80 */                    00000783
   784       IF LENGTH(FLD_DEF)+FLD(F).FLD_COL   > 80 THEN                       00000784
   785       DO;                                                                 00000785
   786          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** ERROR PROCESSING ROW ',FLD(F).FLD_ROW,        00000786
   787                        ' COL ',FLD(F).FLD_COL,': FIELD EXCEEDS COL 80')   00000787
   788                        (A,F(3),A,F(3),A);                                 00000788
   789          RETURN;                                                          00000789
   790       END;                                                                00000790
   791       FLD_NAME = SUBSTR(FLD(F).FLD_NAME||(6)' ',1,6);                     00000791
   792       PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                     00000792
   793           SKIP EDIT('TCMD  CMD=SBA,ROW=',                                 00000793
   794                                   FLD(F).FLD_ROW,',COL=',                 00000794
   795                                   FLD(F).FLD_COL,PANEL_SEQ)               00000795
   796                    (COL(10),A,P'99',A,P'99',COL(73),P'999999V99');        00000796
   797       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                              00000797
   798       LN_PIC = LENGTH(FLD_DEF);                                           00000798
   799       IF LN_PIC = '00' | ATTR_TBL(A).TITLE THEN                           00000799
   800          MACRO_LN = '         TCMD  CMD=SF,MDT=NO';                       00000800
   801       ELSE                                                                00000801
   802          MACRO_LN = FLD_NAME ||'   TCMD  CMD=SF,MDT=YES,LN=' || LN_PIC;   00000802
   803                                                                           00000803
   804       IF FLD(F).PROT THEN                                                 00000804
   805           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',PROT=YES';                             00000805
   806       ELSE                                                                00000806
   807           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',PROT=NO';                              00000807
   808       IF FLD(F).BRIGHT THEN                                               00000808
   809           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',BRIGHT=YES';                           00000809
   810       ELSE                                                                00000810
   811           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',BRIGHT=NO';                            00000811
   812       IF FLD(F).NUM THEN                                                  00000812
   813           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',NUM=YES';                              00000813
   814       ELSE                                                                00000814
   815           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',NUM=NO';                               00000815
   816       IF FLD(F).STOP_BIT &                                                00000816
   817          LENGTH(FLD_DEF)+FLD(F).FLD_COL < 80 THEN                         00000817
   818           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',STOP=YES';                             00000818
   819       ELSE                                                                00000819
   820           MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',STOP=NO';                              00000820

   821                                                                           00000821
   822       IF FLD(F).HI_LIGHT ^= ' ' | FLD(F).COLOR ^= ' ' THEN                00000822

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     27


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   823       DO;                                                                 00000823
   824          MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',';                                      00000824
   825          PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                  00000825
   826                  EDIT(MACRO_LN,'*',PANEL_SEQ) (A,COL(72),A,P'999999V99'); 00000826
   827          PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                           00000827
   828          MACRO_LN = (15)' ';                                              00000828
   829          IF FLD(F).HI_LIGHT = 'U' THEN                                    00000829
   830             MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || 'HILITE=ULN';                          00000830
   831          ELSE                                                             00000831
   832          IF FLD(F).HI_LIGHT = 'R' THEN                                    00000832
   833             MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || 'HILITE=REV';                          00000833
   834          ELSE                                                             00000834
   835          IF FLD(F).HI_LIGHT = 'B' THEN                                    00000835
   836             MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || 'HILITE=BLN';                          00000836
   837          ELSE                                                             00000837
   838          IF FLD(F).HI_LIGHT = 'D' THEN                                    00000838
   839             MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || 'HILITE=DEF';                          00000839
   840          IF FLD(F).HI_LIGHT ^= ' ' & FLD(F).COLOR ^= ' ' THEN             00000840
   841             MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',';                                   00000841
   842          IF FLD(F).COLOR ^= ' ' THEN                                      00000842
   843             MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || 'COLOR=' || FLD(F).COLOR;              00000843
   844       END;                                                                00000844

   845                                                                           00000845
   846       IF LN_PIC = '00' THEN                                               00000846
   847       DO;                                                                 00000847
   848          PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                  00000848
   849                   EDIT(MACRO_LN,PANEL_SEQ) (A,COL(73),P'999999V99');      00000849
   850          PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                           00000850
   851       END;                                                                00000851
   852       ELSE                                                                00000852
   853       DO;                                                                 00000853
   854          MACRO_LN = MACRO_LN || ',';                                      00000854
   855          PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                  00000855
   856                  EDIT(MACRO_LN,'*',PANEL_SEQ) (A,COL(72),A,P'999999V99'); 00000856
   857          PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                           00000857
   858          MACRO_LN = (15)' ' ||'DATA='''||FLD_DEF||'''';                   00000858
   859          IF LENGTH(MACRO_LN)>71 THEN                                      00000859
   860          DO;                                                              00000860
   861             PUT FILE(PANEL)                                               00000861
   862                      EDIT(MACRO_LN,'*',PANEL_SEQ) (A(71),A,P'999999V99')  00000862
   863                        (SUBSTR(MACRO_LN,72),PANEL_SEQ+1)                  00000863
   864                                             (COL(16),A(57),P'999999V99'); 00000864
   865             PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+2;                                        00000865
   866          END;                                                             00000866

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     28


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   867          ELSE                                                             00000867
   868          DO;                                                              00000868
   869             PUT FILE(PANEL)                                               00000869
   870                      EDIT(MACRO_LN,PANEL_SEQ) (A,COL(73),P'999999V99');   00000870
   871          PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                           00000871
   872          END;                                                             00000872
   873       END;                                                                00000873
   874       FLD_DEF='';                                                         00000874
   875    END WRITE_FIELD;                                                       00000875
   876    END WRITE_PANEL;                                                       00000876

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     29


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   877    /*********************************************************************/00000877
   878    /*                                                                   */00000878
   879    /* WRITE_MAPPING - WRITE THE PANEL TO USER FIELD MAPPING             */00000879
   880    /*                                                                   */00000880
   881    /*********************************************************************/00000881
   882    WRITE_MAPPING:PROC;                                                    00000882
   883       DECLARE M FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000883
   884       PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                     00000884
   885                  EDIT(PANEL_NAME||'M','TINPST') (A,COL(10),A)             00000885
   886                      (PANEL_SEQ) (COL(73),P'999999V99');                  00000886
   887       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                              00000887
   888       DO M = 1 TO FLD_CTR;                                                00000888
   889          CALL WRITE_FIELD(M);                                             00000889
   890       END;                                                                00000890
   891       PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                     00000891
   892               EDIT('TINPEND',PANEL_SEQ) (COL(10),A,COL(73),P'999999V99'); 00000892
   893       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                              00000893
   894       PUT FILE(PANEL) EDIT(DT_TIME_STAMP)                    (COL(1),A)   00000894
   895                           (PANEL_SEQ)            (COL(73),P'999999V99');  00000895
   896       PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                              00000896
   897    /****************************************************************/     00000897
   898    WRITE_FIELD:PROC(F);                                                   00000898
   899       DECLARE F FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000899
   900       DECLARE A FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000900
   901       DECLARE MACRO_LN CHAR(160) VARYING;                                 00000901
   902       DECLARE FLD_DEF  CHAR(160) VARYING;                                 00000902
   903       DECLARE FLD_NAME CHAR(8)  VARYING;   /* FORMAT R99C99 */            00000903
   904       A = FLD(F).FLD_ATTR;                                                00000904
   905     /*****                                                                00000905
   906       PUT SKIP DATA(FLD(F));                                              00000906
   907       PUT SKIP DATA(ATTR_TBL(A));                                         00000907
   908     *****/                                                                00000908
   909       FLD_DEF=SUBSTR(FLD(F).FLD_DATA,2);                                  00000909
   910       I = LENGTH(FLD_DEF);                                                00000910
   911       DO WHILE(SUBSTR(FLD_DEF,I,1)=' ' & I>0);                            00000911
   912          I=I-1;                                                           00000912
   913       END;                                                                00000913
   914       IF I=0 THEN FLD_DEF='';                                             00000914
   915       ELSE FLD_DEF=SUBSTR(FLD_DEF,1,I);                                   00000915
   916       IF ^ATTR_TBL(A).TITLE THEN                                          00000916
   917       DO;                                                                 00000917
   918          PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                  00000918
   919                   EDIT(FLD(F).FLD_NAME) (A)                               00000919
   920                       ('TINPMAP ',FLD(F).FLD_ROW,',') (COL(10),A,P'99',A) 00000920
   921                                  (FLD(F).FLD_COL,',',                     00000921

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     30


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   922                                   LENGTH(FLD_DEF)) (P'99',A,P'99')        00000922
   923                         (PANEL_SEQ) (COL(73),P'999999V99');               00000923
   924          PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                           00000924
   925       END;                                                                00000925
   926    END WRITE_FIELD;                                                       00000926
   927    END WRITE_MAPPING;                                                     00000927

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     31


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   928    /*********************************************************************/00000928
   929    /*                                                                   */00000929
   930    /* WRITE_ASM - GENERATE THE USER COMM AREA - ASSEMBLER FORMAT        */00000930
   931    /*                                                                   */00000931
   932    /*********************************************************************/00000932
   933    WRITE_ASM:PROC;                                                        00000933
   934       DECLARE SEQ_NO            FIXED DEC(8,2) INIT(9);                   00000934
   935       PUT FILE(ASM)  EDIT                                                 00000935
   936           (DT_TIME_STAMP,1)               (COL(1),A,COL(73),P'999999V99') 00000936
   937           ('TPARM    DS    0F',2)                (A,COL(73),P'999999V99') 00000937
   938           ('TNAME    DC    CL8''',PANEL_NAME,'''',3)                      00000938
   939                                                       (A,A,A,COL(73),     00000939
   940                                                             P'999999V99') 00000940
   941           ('TADDR    DC    A(0)',4)                   (A,COL(73),         00000941
   942                                                             P'999999V99') 00000942
   943           ('TRC      DC    H''0''',5)                 (A,COL(73),         00000943
   944                                                             P'999999V99') 00000944
   945           ('TAID     DC    X''0''',6)                 (A,COL(73),         00000945
   946                                                             P'999999V99') 00000946
   947           ('TSBA     DC    XL2''0000''',7)            (A,COL(73),         00000947
   948                                                             P'999999V99') 00000948
   949           ('         DC    X''0''',8)                 (A,COL(73),         00000949
   950                                                             P'999999V99');00000950
   951       DO M = 1 TO FLD_CTR;                                                00000951
   952          CALL WRITE_PARM(M);                                              00000952
   953       END;                                                                00000953
   954       PUT FILE(ASM) EDIT                                                  00000954
   955           ('         DC    C'' ''',SEQ_NO)       (A,COL(73),P'999999V99') 00000955
   956           ('         DC    AL2(0)',SEQ_NO+1)     (A,COL(73),P'999999V99') 00000956
   957           (DT_TIME_STAMP,SEQ_NO+2)        (COL(1),A,COL(73),P'999999V99');00000957
   958       SEQ_NO=SEQ_NO+3;                                                    00000958
   959    WRITE_PARM:PROC(F);                                                    00000959
   960       DECLARE F FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000960
   961       DECLARE A FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000961
   962       DECLARE I FIXED BIN(15);                                            00000962
   963       DECLARE MACRO_LN CHAR(160) VARYING;                                 00000963
   964       DECLARE LN_PIC   PIC '99';                                          00000964
   965       DECLARE FLD_DEF  CHAR(160) VARYING;                                 00000965
   966       DECLARE FLD_NAME CHAR(160) VARYING;                                 00000966
   967       A = FLD(F).FLD_ATTR;                                                00000967
   968     /*****                                                                00000968
   969       PUT SKIP DATA(FLD(F));                                              00000969
   970       PUT SKIP DATA(ATTR_TBL(A));                                         00000970
   971     *****/                                                                00000971
   972       FLD_DEF=SUBSTR(FLD(F).FLD_DATA,2);                                  00000972

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     32


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   973       I = LENGTH(FLD_DEF);                                                00000973
   974       DO WHILE(SUBSTR(FLD_DEF,I,1)=' ' & I>0);                            00000974
   975          I=I-1;                                                           00000975
   976       END;                                                                00000976
   977       IF I=0 THEN FLD_DEF='';                                             00000977
   978       ELSE FLD_DEF=SUBSTR(FLD_DEF,1,I);                                   00000978
   979       /* MAKE SURE THAT FIELDS DON'T GO PAST COL 80 */                    00000979
   980       IF LENGTH(FLD_DEF)+FLD(F).FLD_COL   > 80 THEN                       00000980
   981       DO;                                                                 00000981
   982          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** ERROR PROCESSING ROW ',FLD(F).FLD_ROW,        00000982
   983                        ' COL ',FLD(F).FLD_COL,': FIELD EXCEEDS COL 80')   00000983
   984                        (A,F(3),A,F(3),A);                                 00000984
   985          RETURN;                                                          00000985
   986       END;                                                                00000986
   987       FLD_NAME = FLD(F).FLD_NAME;                                         00000987
   988       LN_PIC = LENGTH(FLD_DEF);                                           00000988
   989       IF LN_PIC ^= '00' & ^ATTR_TBL(A).TITLE THEN                         00000989

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     39


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

   INCLUDED TEXT FOLLOWS FROM DD.MEMBER =  SYSLIB  .SELECT

  1282    /********************************************************************* 00000001
  1283                                                                           00000002
  1284      THE SELECT, WHEN AND OTHERWISE MACROS FOR USE WITH PL/I (F).         00000003
  1285                                                                           00000004
  1286      THESE MACROS EMULATE THE PL/I SELECT STATEMENT WHICH WAS NOT         00000005
  1287      IMPLEMENTED IN THE PL/I (F) COMPILER.                                00000006
  1288                                                                           00000007
  1289      TO USE, %INCLUDE THIS MEMBER IN YOUR PROGRAM AND COMPILE WITH        00000008
  1290      THE MACRO OPTION. (NOMACRO IS THE DEFAULT).                          00000009
  1291                                                                           00000010
  1292      CODE THE SELECT:                                                     00000011
  1293                                                                           00000012
  1294          SELECT (A)                 SELECT (TRUE)                         00000013
  1295          WHEN(1)                    WHEN(A=1)                             00000014
  1296            CALL SUB1;                 CALL SUB1;                          00000015
  1297          WHEN(X)                    WHEN(A=X)                             00000016
  1298          DO;                        DO;                                   00000017
  1299            CALL XRTN(X);              CALL XTRN(X);                       00000018
  1300            X=X+A;                     X=X+A;                              00000019
  1301          END;                       END;                                  00000020
  1302          OTHERWISE                  OTHERWISE                             00000021
  1303          END;                       END;                                  00000022
  1304                                                                           00000023
  1305      NOTE - USING THE MACROS, THE OTHERWISE IS REQUIRED, EVEN IF THE      00000024
  1306          STATEMENT TO EXECUTE IS NULL.                                    00000025
  1307                                                                           00000026
  1308    **********************************************************************/00000027
  1309                                                                           00000028
  1310                                                                           00000029
  1311    %DECLARE                                                               00000030
  1312        SELECT    ENTRY (CHARACTER) RETURNS (CHARACTER),                   00000031
  1313        WHEN      ENTRY (CHARACTER) RETURNS (CHARACTER),                   00000032
  1314        OTHERWISE ENTRY             RETURNS (CHARACTER);                   00000033
  1315    %DECLARE                                                               00000034
  1316         WHEN_CTR            FIXED,                                        00000035
  1317        (SELEXPR,SPACES)     CHARACTER;                                    00000036
  1318      %WHEN_CTR = 0;                                                       00000037
  1319      %SPACES = '                                                          00000038
  1320                ';                                                         00000039
  1321    %SELECT :                                                              00000040
  1322        PROCEDURE (A) RETURNS (CHARACTER);                                 00000041
  1323                                                                           00000042
  1324          DECLARE  (A,L1,L2) CHARACTER;                                    00000043

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     40


   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

  1325                                                                           00000044
  1326          IF WHEN_CTR > 0 THEN                                             00000045
  1327              RETURN('/*** THE SELECT MACRO CANNOT BE NESTED ***/');       00000046
  1328                                                                           00000047
  1329          SELEXPR = A;                                                     00000048
  1330          WHEN_CTR = 1;                                                    00000049
  1331                                                                           00000050
  1332          L1 = '/* SELECT (' || SELEXPR || ') */';                         00000051
  1333          L2 = 'DO;              /* START OF SELECT EMULATION */';         00000052
  1334                                                                           00000053
  1335          L1 = SUBSTR(L1||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000054
  1336          L2 = SUBSTR(L2||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000055
  1337                                                                           00000056
  1338          RETURN(L1||L2);                                                  00000057
  1339    %END;                                                                  00000058
  1340                                                                           00000059
  1341    %WHEN :                                                                00000060
  1342        PROCEDURE (A) RETURNS (CHARACTER);                                 00000061
  1343                                                                           00000062
  1344          DECLARE  (A,L1,L2,L3,L4,L5) CHARACTER;                           00000063
  1345                                                                           00000064
  1346          IF WHEN_CTR > 1 THEN                                             00000065
  1347          DO;                                                              00000066
  1348             L1='END;';                                                    00000067
  1349             L2='/* WHEN (' || A || '); */';                               00000068
  1350             L3='ELSE';                                                    00000069
  1351          END;                                                             00000070
  1352          ELSE                                                             00000071
  1353          IF WHEN_CTR = 1 THEN                                             00000072
  1354          DO;                                                              00000073
  1355             L1=' ';                                                       00000074
  1356             L2='/* WHEN (' || A || '); */';                               00000075
  1357             L3=' ';                                                       00000076
  1358          END;                                                             00000077
  1359          ELSE                                                             00000078
  1360             RETURN('/** WHEN WITHOUT A SELECT **/');                      00000079
  1361                                                                           00000080
  1362          WHEN_CTR = WHEN_CTR + 1;                                         00000081
  1363                                                                           00000082
  1364          IF SELEXPR = 'TRUE' THEN                                         00000083
  1365          L4='IF (' || A || ') THEN';                                      00000084
  1366          ELSE                                                             00000085
  1367          L4='IF (' || SELEXPR || ')=(' || A || ') THEN';                  00000086
  1368          L5='DO;';                                                        00000087
  1369                                                                           00000088

   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

  1370          L1 = SUBSTR(L1||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000089
  1371          L2 = SUBSTR(L2||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000090
  1372          L3 = SUBSTR(L3||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000091
  1373          L4 = SUBSTR(L4||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000092
  1374          L5 = SUBSTR(L5||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000093
  1375                                                                           00000094
  1376          RETURN(L1||L2||L3||L4||L5);                                      00000095
  1377    %END ;                                                                 00000096
  1378                                                                           00000097
  1379    %OTHERWISE :                                                           00000098
  1380        PROCEDURE RETURNS (CHARACTER);                                     00000099
  1381                                                                           00000100
  1382          DECLARE  (L1,L2,L3) CHARACTER;                                   00000101
  1383                                                                           00000102
  1384          IF WHEN_CTR < 1 THEN                                             00000103
  1385             RETURN('/** OTHERWISE OUT OF SEQUENCE **/');                  00000104
  1386                                                                           00000105
  1387          WHEN_CTR = 0;                                                    00000106
  1388                                                                           00000107
  1389          L1='END;';                                                       00000108
  1390          L2='/* OTHERWISE */';                                            00000109
  1391          L3='ELSE';                                                       00000110
  1392                                                                           00000111

  1394          L2 = SUBSTR(L2||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000113
  1395          L3 = SUBSTR(L3||SPACES,1,71);                                    00000114
  1396                                                                           00000115
  1397          RETURN(L1||L2||L3);                                              00000116
  1398    %END;                                                                  00000117
  1399                                                                           00000118

   STMT LEVEL NEST
                     /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/    1
                     /*********************************************************************/    2
                     /*                                                                   */    3
                     /* NAME: MAP3270 - SCREEN COMPILER                                   */    4
                     /*                                                                   */    5
                     /*********************************************************************/    6
                     /*                                                                   */    7
                     /*  (C) COPYRIGHT 2009  CEDAR LAKE EMPORIUM LLC   ALL RIGHTS RESERVED*/    8
                     /*  (C) COPYRIGHT 2010  CEDAR LAKE EMPORIUM LLC   ALL RIGHTS RESERVED*/    9
                     /*                                                                   */   10
                     /*  THIS SOURCE CODE AS WELL AS ANY OBJECT CODE RESULTING FROM THIS  */   11
                     /*  SOURCE CODE MAY BE DISTRIBUTED FREELY PROVIDED NO FEE IS CHARGED */   12
                     /*  AND FOR NON-COMERCIAL PURPOSES.                                  */   13
                     /*                                                                   */   14
                     /*  FOR COMMERCIAL DISTRIBUTION RIGHTS, CONTACT THE COPYRIGHT OWNER. */   15
                     /*                                                                   */   16
                     /*********************************************************************/   17
                     /*                                                                   */   18
                     /* THIS IS A PROGRAM TO PROCESS A SCREEN DEFINITION FILE AND CREATES */   19
                     /* A PANEL FOR THE MAP3270 SYSTEM.                                   */   20
                     /*                                                                   */   21
                     /* A PANEL FOR THE MAP3270 SYSTEM CONSISTS OF 2 COMPONENTS - A       */   22
                     /* PHYSICAL MAP AND A USER MAP.  CONCEPTUALLY THESE ARE LIKE CICS    */   23
                     /* PHYSICAL AND SYMBOLIC MAPS.  HOWEVER, THERE IS NO COMPATABILITY.  */   24
                     /*                                                                   */   25
                     /* THE PHYSICAL MAP IS CONSISTS OF AN INDEX, THE ACTUAL 3270 MAP     */   26
                     /* AND THE CROSS REFERENCE FROM THE PHYSICAL MAP TO A USER MAP.      */   27
                     /* THE USER MAP IS THE AREA THAT USER'S APPLICATION SENDS AND        */   28
                     /* RECEIVES DATA FROM MAP3270 RUNTIME MODULES.                       */   29
                     /*                                                                   */   30
                     /* USER MAPS ARE GENERATED FOR ASSEMBLER, COBOL, AND PL/I (F).       */   31
                     /* THE PHYSICAL MAP IS GENERATED AND MUST BE ASSEMLED AND LINKED.    */   32
                     /*                                                                   */   33
                     /* REVISION HISTORY                                                  */   34
                     /* ------  --------------------------------------------------------  */   35
                     /* V2.0.0  "DOWNGRADED" FROM PL/1 OPTIMIZING COMPILER TO PL/1 (F)    */   36
                     /*         SEPT 2008                                                 */   37
                     /* V2.1.0  ADDED SUPPORT FOR THE EXTENTED ATTRIBUTES HIGHLITE AND    */   38
                     /*         COLOR.                                                    */   39
                     /*         REWORKED CODE TO USE THE SELECT...WHEN  MACRO, WHICH      */   40
                     /*         SIMULATES THE SELECT STATEMENT.                           */   41
                     /*         AUGUST 2010                                               */   42

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     43


   STMT LEVEL NEST

                     /*                                                                   */   43
                     /*********************************************************************/   44
                     /*********************************************************************  1282
                                                                                             1282
                       THE SELECT, WHEN AND OTHERWISE MACROS FOR USE WITH PL/I (F).          1282
                                                                                             1282
                       THESE MACROS EMULATE THE PL/I SELECT STATEMENT WHICH WAS NOT          1282
                       IMPLEMENTED IN THE PL/I (F) COMPILER.                                 1282
                                                                                             1282
                       TO USE, %INCLUDE THIS MEMBER IN YOUR PROGRAM AND COMPILE WITH         1282
                       THE MACRO OPTION. (NOMACRO IS THE DEFAULT).                           1282
                                                                                             1282
                       CODE THE SELECT:                                                      1282
                                                                                             1282
                           SELECT (A)                 SELECT (TRUE)                          1282
                           WHEN(1)                    WHEN(A=1)                              1282
                             CALL SUB1;                 CALL SUB1;                           1282
                           WHEN(X)                    WHEN(A=X)                              1282
                           DO;                        DO;                                    1282
                             CALL XRTN(X);              CALL XTRN(X);                        1282
                             X=X+A;                     X=X+A;                               1282
                           END;                       END;                                   1282
                           OTHERWISE                  OTHERWISE                              1282
                           END;                       END;                                   1282
                                                                                             1282
                       NOTE - USING THE MACROS, THE OTHERWISE IS REQUIRED, EVEN IF THE       1282
                           STATEMENT TO EXECUTE IS NULL.                                     1282
                                                                                             1282
                     **********************************************************************/ 1282
                                                                                             1308
                                                                                             1310
                                                                                             1340
                                                                                             1378
                                                                                             1399
                     /*********************************************************************/ 1400

                     /*********************************************************************/  123
                     /*                                                                   */  124
                     /* READ AND LIST THE INPUT STATEMENTS.  SET UP THE PAGE HEADING      */  125
                     /*    SET UP THE PAGE HEADING.  THEN THE INPUT IS LISTED AND PARSED  */  126
                     /*    INPUT CONSISTS OF SECTIONS AND COMMAND.  EACH SECTION STARTS   */  127
                     /*    WITH '.NAME ' IN COL 1.  VALID NAMES ARE LISTED BELOW.         */  128
                     /*    COMMAND START WITH '.KW=' IN COL 1.                            */  129
                     /*                                                                   */  130
                     /* THERE ARE 3 SECTIONS                                              */  131
                     /* 1.  ATTR - THIS IS WHERE THE ATTRIBUTES ARE DEFINED. THESE MUST   */  132
                     /*     BE DEFINED BEFORE USE IN THE SCREEN SECTION.                  */  133
                     /* 2.  SCREEN - THIS IS WHERE THE 'DRAWING' OF THE SCREEN IS         */  134
                     /*     IS DEFINED.  EACH FIELD BEGIN WITH AN ATTRIBUTED AS DEFINED   */  135
                     /*     IN THE ATTR SECTION.                                          */  136
                     /* 3.  VARS - THIS OPTIONAL SECTION MAPS ANY USER DEFINED FIELD      */  137
                     /*     NAME TO BE DEFINED.  THESE NAME REPLACE THE DEFAULT NAME OF   */  138
                     /*     R99C99.                                                       */  139
                     /*                                                                   */  140
                     /* THE FOLLOWING IS A LIST OF COMMAND CURRENTLY SUPPORTED:           */  141
                     /*                                                                   */  142
                     /* 1.  .NAME= THIS COMMAND SETS THE NAME FOR THE PANEL.  NAME CAN    */  143
                     /*     BE ANY VALID NAME 1-7 CHARACTERS.  MAP3270 GENERATES SOME     */  144
                     /*     INTERNAL NAMES USING 'NAME' PLUS 1 CHARACTER.                 */  145
                     /*                                                                   */  146
                     /*********************************************************************/  147
                                                                                              148
