           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     61


   STMT LEVEL NEST

                     /*********************************************************************/  484
                     /*                                                                   */  485
                     /*   THIS ROUTINE PROCESSES ALL OF THE VARS LINES.  THE GENERAL      */  486
                     /*   FORMAT IS:                                                      */  487
                     /*   R99C99=NAME123,ATTR,ATTR COMMENTS                               */  488
                     /*   R99C99 IS THE NAME GENERATED BY MAP3270.                        */  489
                     /*   NAME IS 1 TO 7 CHARACTER NAME ASSIGNED BY THE PROGRAMMER.       */  490
                     /*   ,ATTR IS AN ADDITIONAL OR OVERRIDE ATTRIBUTE FOR THIS FIELD.    */  491
                     /*         0 OR MORE ATTRS MAY BE SPECIFIED.  THE LIST ENDS WHEN     */  492
                     /*         THE FIRST SPACE IS ENCOUNTERED.                           */  493
                     /*                                                                   */  494
                     /*********************************************************************/  495
                                                                                              496
   329     1         PROCESS_VARS:PROC;                                                       497
   330     2            DECLARE (MATCH_INI_NAME,MATCH_NAME) BIT(1) ALIGNED;                   498
   331     2            DECLARE (TEMP,TEMP2)        CHAR(78) VARYING;                         499
   332     2            DECLARE (I,COMMA,BLANK,NST,NLEN) FIXED BINARY(15) ALIGNED;            500
   333     2            DECLARE (FLD_NAME_PTR)           FIXED BINARY(15) ALIGNED;            501
   334     2            IF SUBSTR(MY_REC,7,1)^='=' THEN                                       502
   335     2            DO;                                                                   503
   336     2    1          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** EXPECTED ''='' NOT FOUND ***') (A);             504
   337     2    1          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                                505
   338     2    1          RETURN;                                                            506
   339     2    1       END;                                                                  507
   340     2            COMMA=INDEX(MY_REC,',');                                              508
   341     2            BLANK=INDEX(MY_REC,' ');                                              509
   342     2            NST=8;                                                                510
                         /* SELECT (TRUE) */                                                  511 1
   343     2             DO;              /* START OF SELECT EMULATION */                     511 1
   344     2    1         ;                                                                   511 1
                                                                                              512 1
                            /* WHEN (COMMA=0 & BLANK>0); */                                   512 1
                                                                                              512 1
   345     2    1           IF (COMMA=0 & BLANK>0) THEN                                       512 1
   346     2    1           DO;                                                               512 1
                               /* NO COMMA FOUND BUT A BLANK WAS */                           512 1
   347     2    2              NLEN=BLANK-NST;                                                513
   348     2    2           END;                                                              514 1
                            /* WHEN (BLANK=0 & COMMA>0); */                                   514 1
   349     2    1           ELSE                                                              514 1
   349     2    1           IF (BLANK=0 & COMMA>0) THEN                                       514 1
   350     2    1           DO;                                                               514 1
                                 /* NO BLANK FOUND BUT A COMMA WAS */                         514 1
   351     2    2              NLEN=COMMA-NST;                                                515
   352     2    2           END;                                                              516 1

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     62


   STMT LEVEL NEST

                            /* WHEN (COMMA<BLANK); */                                         516 1
   353     2    1           ELSE                                                              516 1
   353     2    1           IF (COMMA<BLANK) THEN                                             516 1
   354     2    1           DO;                                                               516 1
                                 /* ATTR STARTS BEFORE BLANK       */                         516 1
   355     2    2              NLEN=COMMA-NST;                                                517
   356     2    2           END;                                                              518 1
                            /* WHEN (COMMA>BLANK); */                                         518 1
   357     2    1           ELSE                                                              518 1
   357     2    1           IF (COMMA>BLANK) THEN                                             518 1
   358     2    1           DO;                                                               518 1
                                 /* BLANK APPEARS BEFORE COMMA     */                         518 1
   359     2    2              NLEN=BLANK-NST;                                                519
   360     2    2           END;                                                              520 1
                            /* OTHERWISE */                                                   520 1
   361     2    1           ELSE                                                              520 1
                                                                                              520 1
   361     2    1          DO;                                                                521
   362     2    2             PUT SKIP EDIT('*** LOGIC ERROR 1 ***') (A);                     522
   363     2    2             ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                             523
   364     2    2             RETURN;                                                         524
   365     2    2          END;                                                               525
   366     2    1       IF NLEN>7 THEN                                                        526
   367     2    1       DO;                                                                   527
   368     2    2          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** INCORRECT FIELD LENGTHS ***') (A);              528
   369     2    2          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                                529
   370     2    2          RETURN;                                                            530
   371     2    2       END;                                                                  531
   372     2    1       DO I = 1 TO VAR_CTR;                                                  532
   373     2    2          IF VAR(I).VAR_NAME = SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6) THEN                       533
   374     2    2          DO;                                                                534
   375     2    3              PUT SKIP EDIT('*** DUPLICATE VAR NAME ',VAR(I).VAR_NAME,       535
                                            ' ***') (A,A,A);                                  536
   376     2    3              ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                            537
   377     2    3              RETURN;                                                        538
   378     2    3          END;                                                               539
   379     2    2          IF VAR(I).VAR_FLD = SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST,NLEN) THEN                   540
   380     2    2          DO;                                                                541
   381     2    3              PUT SKIP EDIT('*** DUPLICATE VAR FIELD ',                      542
                                             SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST,NLEN),' ***') (A,A,A);         543
   382     2    3              ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                            544
   383     2    3              RETURN;                                                        545
   384     2    3          END;                                                               546
   385     2    2       END;                                                                  547
   386     2    1       MATCH_INI_NAME=FALSE;                                                 548

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     63


   STMT LEVEL NEST

   387     2    1       MATCH_NAME=FALSE;                                                     549
   388     2    1       FLD_NAME_PTR=0;                                                       550
   389     2    1       DO WHILE(FLD_NAME_PTR<FLD_CTR & ^MATCH_INI_NAME);                     551
   390     2    2          FLD_NAME_PTR=FLD_NAME_PTR+1;                                       552
   391     2    2          MATCH_INI_NAME =                                                   553
                                 (FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).FLD_INT_NAME = SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6));       554
   392     2    2       END;                                                                  555
   393     2    1       IF MATCH_INI_NAME THEN ;                                              556
   395     2    1       ELSE                                                                  557
   395     2    1       DO;                                                                   558
   396     2    2          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** INTERNAL NAME NOT DEFINED ',                    559
                                         SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6),                                  560
                                         ' ***') (A,A,A);                                     561
   397     2    2          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                                562
   398     2    2          RETURN;                                                            563
   399     2    2       END;                                                                  564
   400     2    1       VAR_CTR=VAR_CTR+1;                                                    565
   401     2    1       VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_NAME=SUBSTR(MY_REC,1,6);                             566
   402     2    1       VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_FLD=SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST,NLEN);                         567
   403     2    1       I=INDEX(VAR(VAR_CTR).VAR_FLD,' ');                                    568
   404     2    1       IF I=0 THEN ;               /* NAME HAS NO SPACES - IT IS OK */       569
   406     2    1       ELSE                                                                  570
   406     2    1       IF I=1 THEN                                                           571
   407     2    1       DO;                                                                   572
   408     2    2          PUT SKIP EDIT('*** USER DEFINED NAME IS BLANK ***') (A);           573
   409     2    2          ERROR_FOUND = TRUE;                                                574
   410     2    2          RETURN;                                                            575
   411     2    2       END;                                                                  576
   412     2    1       IF COMMA=0 | BLANK<COMMA THEN    /* NO ATTRIBUTES */                  577
   413     2    1           RETURN;                                                           578
   414     2    1       TEMP,TEMP2 = SUBSTR(MY_REC,NST+NLEN+1);  /* GET RID OF NAME */        579
   415     2    1       BLANK=INDEX(TEMP,' ');                                                580
   416     2    1       IF BLANK>0 THEN TEMP,TEMP2=SUBSTR(TEMP,1,BLANK-1);                    581
   418     2    1       FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).ATTR_A=FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).ATTR_A||'<'||TEMP2||'>';   582
   419     2    1       I=1;                                                                  583
   420     2    1       DO WHILE(I>0);                                                        584
   421     2    2          I=INDEX(TEMP,',');                                                 585
   422     2    2          IF I>0 THEN                                                        586
   423     2    2          DO;                                                                587
   424     2    3             CALL CHECK_ATTR(SUBSTR(TEMP,1,I-1),FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).FLD_REC);  588
   425     2    3             TEMP=SUBSTR(TEMP,I+1);                                          589
   426     2    3          END;                                                               590
   427     2    2          ELSE                                                               591
   427     2    2             CALL CHECK_ATTR(TEMP,FLD(FLD_NAME_PTR).FLD_REC);                592
   428     2    2       END;                                                                  593

                     /****************************************************************/       598
   431     1         PROCESS_SCREEN:PROC;                                                     599
                                                                                              600
   432     2            DECLARE (C,I               ) FIXED BINARY(15),                        601
                                 K                   CHAR(1);                                 602
   433     2            NO_ATTRIB = TRUE;                                                     603
   434     2            ROW = ROW + 1;                               /* COUNT ROW WE ARE  */  604
   435     2            B = B + 1; SCR_IMG(B) = '* ' || MY_REC;                               605
   437     2            COL = 1;                                                              606
   438     2            FLD_A = 1;                                                            607
   439     2            DO C = 1 TO 80;                              /* PROCESS ONE BY ONE*/  608
   440     2    1          K = SUBSTR(MY_REC,C,1);                   /* GET NEXT BYTE     */  609
   441     2    1          DO I = 1 TO A;                            /* TEST IF ATTRIBUTE */  610
   442     2    2             IF ATTR_TBL(I).ATTR_CHR = K THEN       /* IF WE FIND AN     */  611
   443     2    2             DO;                                    /*  ATTRIBUTE        */  612
   444     2    3                NO_ATTRIB = FALSE;                                           613
   445     2    3                IF FLD_DEF  ^= '' THEN              /* AND WE ALREADY    */  614
   446     2    3                DO;                                                          615
   447     2    4                    CALL SAVE_FIELD(FLD_A);         /*  HAVE DATA        */  616
   448     2    4                    FLD_DEF = '';                                            617
   449     2    4                END;                                                         618
   450     2    3                COL = C;                                                     619
   451     2    3                FLD_A = I;                                                   620
   452     2    3             END; /* IF */                                                   621
   453     2    2          END; /* DO */                                                      622
                        /* IF NO_ATTRIB THEN  ;                                               623
                           ELSE                                                               623
                        */                                                                    623
   454     2    1     DO;                                                                     625
   455     2    2             FLD_DEF = FLD_DEF  || K;                                        626
                             /*  IF SUBSTR(X,C,1)= '''' THEN DATA = DATA  ''''  */          627
   456     2    2          END;                                                               628
   457     2    1       END; /* DO */                                                         629

   459     2            DO;                                                                   631

   461     2    1          FLD_DEF = '';                                                      633
   462     2    1       END;                                                                  634

                     /*********************************************************************/  652

                     /* PRINT_ATTR - PRINT ATTRIBUTES FOR A GIVEN FIELD                   */  654

   477     1         PRINT_ATTR:PROC(ATTR);                                                   657
   478     2            DECLARE ATTR LIKE ATTR_REC;                                           658
   479     2               IF ATTR.TITLE THEN                                                 659
   480     2                  PUT EDIT('TITLE ') (A);                                         660
                                                                                              661
   481     2               IF ATTR.NUM THEN PUT EDIT('NUM ') (A);                             662
   483     2               ELSE PUT EDIT('ALPHA ') (A);                                       663
                                                                                              664

   486     2               ELSE PUT EDIT('UNPROT ') (A);                                      666
                                                                                              667

   489     2               ELSE PUT EDIT('NORMAL ') (A);                                      669
                                                                                              670
                            /* SELECT (ATTR.HI_LIGHT) */                                      671 1
   490     2                DO;              /* START OF SELECT EMULATION */                  671 1
                                                                                              671 1
                                                                                              672 1
                                /* WHEN (' '); */                                             672 1
                                                                                              672 1
   491     2    1               IF (ATTR.HI_LIGHT)=(' ') THEN                                 672 1
   492     2    1               DO;                                                           672 1
   493     2    2                  ;                                                          672 1
   494     2    2               END;                                                          673 1
                                /* WHEN ('D'); */                                             673 1
   495     2    1               ELSE                                                          673 1
   495     2    1               IF (ATTR.HI_LIGHT)=('D') THEN                                 673 1
   496     2    1               DO;                                                           673 1
   497     2    2                  PUT EDIT('HI DEFAULT ') (A);                               673 1
   498     2    2               END;                                                          674 1
                                /* WHEN ('U'); */                                             674 1
   499     2    1               ELSE                                                          674 1
   499     2    1               IF (ATTR.HI_LIGHT)=('U') THEN                                 674 1
   500     2    1               DO;                                                           674 1
   501     2    2                  PUT EDIT('UNDERLINE ') (A);                                674 1
   502     2    2               END;                                                          675 1
                                /* WHEN ('R'); */                                             675 1
   503     2    1               ELSE                                                          675 1
   503     2    1               IF (ATTR.HI_LIGHT)=('R') THEN                                 675 1
   504     2    1               DO;                                                           675 1

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     68


   STMT LEVEL NEST

   505     2    2                  PUT EDIT('REVERSE ') (A);                                  675 1
   506     2    2               END;                                                          676 1
                                /* WHEN ('B'); */                                             676 1
   507     2    1               ELSE                                                          676 1
   507     2    1               IF (ATTR.HI_LIGHT)=('B') THEN                                 676 1
   508     2    1               DO;                                                           676 1
   509     2    2                  PUT EDIT('BLINK ') (A);                                    676 1
   510     2    2               END;                                                          677 1

   511     2    1               ELSE                                                          677 1

                     /*********************************************************************/  689
                     /*                                                                   */  690
                     /* WRITE_PANEL - WRITE THE MACROS TO GENERATE THE PANEL              */  691
                     /*                                                                   */  692
                     /* IN THE MAP3270 SYSTEM, THE PANEL IS A LOAD MODULE GENERATED FROM  */  693
                     /* ASSEMBLER CODE GENERATED BY THIS PROGRAM.  THE PANEL HAS 3        */  694
                     /* SECTIONS:                                                         */  695
                     /*    1) INDEX TO THE  DATA STREAM, CROSS REFERENCE AND INSERT       */  696
                     /*       CURSOR AREAS.                                               */  697
                     /*    2) 3270 DATA STEAM WHICH CONTAINS THE INSERT CURSOR STUFF.     */  698
                     /*    3) CROSS REFERENCE WHICH MAPS THE FIELDS IN THE DATA STREAM    */  699
                     /*       TO THE USER MAP.                                            */  700
                     /*                                                                   */  701
                     /*********************************************************************/  702
   522     1         WRITE_PANEL:PROC;                                                        703
   523     2            DECLARE M FIXED BIN(15);                                              704
   524     2            DECLARE IC_WRITTEN  BIT(1) ALIGNED;                                   705
                                                                                              706
   525     2            OPEN FILE(PANEL) TITLE('MAP');                                        707
                                                                                              708
   526     2            PUT FILE(PANEL) EDIT('TITLE ''PANEL ',PANEL_NAME,' ',                 709
                                             TITLE_STAMP,'''')     (COL(10),A,A,A,A,A)        710
                                            (PANEL_SEQ)            (COL(73),P'999999V99');    711
   527     2            PANE_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+1;                                                 712
   528     2            PUT FILE(PANEL) EDIT(DT_TIME_STAMP)                    (COL(1),A)     713
                                            (PANEL_SEQ)            (COL(73),P'999999V99')     714
                                            (PANEL_NAME,'TSECT')            (A,COL(10),A)     715
                                            (PANEL_SEQ+1)          (COL(73),P'999999V99')     716
                                            ('DC    A(', PANEL_NAME||'P)' ) (COL(10),A,A)     717
                                            (PANEL_SEQ+2)          (COL(73),P'999999V99')     718
                                            ('DC    A(', PANEL_NAME||'M)' ) (COL(10),A,A)     719
                                            (PANEL_SEQ+3)          (COL(73),P'999999V99')     720
                                            ('DC    A(', PANEL_NAME||'C)' ) (COL(10),A,A)     721
                                            (PANEL_SEQ+4)          (COL(73),P'999999V99');    722
   529     2            PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+5;                                                723
   530     2            PUT FILE(PANEL)                                                       724
                                   EDIT(PANEL_NAME,'TSTPAN',PANEL_SEQ)                        725
                                                        (A,COL(10),A,COL(73),P'999999V99')    726
                                       ('TWCC  RESET=YES,RSTMDT=YES',PANEL_SEQ+1)             727
                                                          (COL(10),A,COL(73),P'999999V99');   728
   531     2            PANEL_SEQ=PANEL_SEQ+2;                                                729
   532     2            IC_WRITTEN=FALSE;                                                     730
   533     2            M = FLD_CTR;                                                          731
   534     2            DO WHILE (M>0);                                                       732
   535     2    1          IF ATTR_TBL(FLD(M).FLD_ATTR).CUR THEN                              733

           /********************** MAP3270 V2.1.0********************************/00000001                  PAGE     70



   STMT LEVEL NEST

   536     2    1          DO;                                                                734
   537     2    2             CALL WRITE_IC(FLD(M).FLD_ROW,FLD(M).FLD_COL);                   735
   538     2    2             IC_WRITTEN=TRUE;                                                736

   540     2    2          END;                                                               738
